Prompt 1 (Pixel Art Game Icon):
This character is depicted as a 16-bit RPG icon in a dramatic wide shot, styled like a pixel-art Nintendo character from a cinematic game sequence. He stands in a calm yet battle-ready stance, his full body centered against a crumbling gothic cathedral backdrop under a swirling violet sky. His dirty blonde hair is tousled, his icy blue eyes narrowed with stern intensity. He wears a long navy duster coat with bronze trim over a dark vest, a silver-winged brooch glowing faintly on his lapel. His right arm is encased in a segmented silver gauntlet, his left in a simple leather glove. Dark trousers tuck into knee-high combat boots. He grips his colossal greatsword, its blade channeling pulsing blue energy from a skull-etched hilt, resting the tip on the ground as ethereal azure aura wisps curl around his pale ivory features.

The intricate details of his navy duster's bronze trim, the glowing winged brooch on his lapel, and the segmented silver gauntlet on his right arm are rendered in stunning clarity. A faint, otherworldly aura shimmers around his broad shoulders, hinting at latent arcane power.

He stands in a calm yet battle-ready stance, his lean agile feline-hourglass figure centered on a grand elevated plaza of pristine white marble and gold-inlaid stone circles beneath massive soaring arches and slender spires reaching toward a soft dawn-lit sky, giant ornamental swords embedded in guardrails draped with fluttering blue banners. His brilliant snowy white hair is styled in a wild windswept fashion with thick jagged tufts flaring outward and upward including a prominent central fringe sweeping across his forehead, two large pointed slate-grey cat ears with soft inner tufts emerging from his crown. His fair porcelain-smooth skin features a soft rounded jawline retaining boyishness and a small straight delicate nose, his large expressive eyes shimmering with vibrant deep violet amethyst hue suggesting latent magical power. He wears a high-collared sleeveless white mantle with golden embroidered trim and distinct blue lining draping over his shoulders over a rich cerulean blue short-sleeved tunic fitting snugly to his agile frame. A sturdy dark brown leather utility belt with large ornate silver buckle secures pouches and his magical catalyst. Asymmetrical bracers protect his arms—a thick leather gauntlet with metallic reinforcement on his right, a decorative silver-winged pauldron humming with energy on his left shoulder. Loose-fitting charcoal-grey trousers tuck into specialized brown leather greaves with golden accents and straps wrapping his calves, sandal-style footwear with dark soles and sturdy straps allowing feline agility. A long slender slate-grey feline tail emerges from his trousers providing balance. His primary weapon is a sophisticated floating magical orb of polished silver and gold glowing with pulsing blue light holstered near his belt, pixelated disciplined blue energy ripples and crystalline sparks trailing behind him suggesting mastery over space-time.

His fair porcelain-smooth flawless skin catches the golden dawn light. The high-collared sleeveless white mantle with golden embroidered trim and blue lining drapes over his shoulders above the rich cerulean blue short-sleeved tunic, the sturdy dark brown utility belt with ornate silver buckle visible at his waist. The decorative silver-winged pauldron on his left shoulder hums with subtle energy as one hand rests near the floating magical orb of polished silver and gold pulsing with blue light, faint ripples of disciplined energy and crystalline sparks drifting around him suggesting temporal manipulation mastery.

Intricate articulated gauntlets protect his hands, sleek greaves and sabatons tapering to sharp pointed toes armor his lower body. A heavy dual-toned cape of deep crimson interior and midnight black exterior drapes from his shoulders, tattered at the hem. In his hands, he grips a massive two-handed claymore with exceptionally long slender shimmering silver blade transitioning to translucent glowing cyan toward the edges, its hilt featuring a jagged cross-guard matching his armor, the entire weapon pulsing with rhythmic ghostly aura. Beside him stands his warhorse with dark matte charcoal coat, its mane and tail composed of flowing ethereal spirit-fire in brilliant pale turquoise, armored in silver plates with bladed chanfron, its eyes glowing supernatural blue, pixelated cold stoic aura and spectral particles swirling around this tragic knight and his ethereal mount.
